from \"../services/password-reset.service.js\";\n\n// Types for route context\ntype AuthContext = {\n  keyId: string;\n  role?: string;\n  scope?: string;\n  sessionId?: string;\n};\n\n// ============================================================================\n// In-Memory User Storage (Replace with database in production)\n// ============================================================================\n\n/**\n * Simple in-memory user storage.\n * In production, this would be a database table with:\n * - userId (primary key)\n * - email (unique)\n * - passwordHash\n * - passwordSalt\n * - createdAt\n * - updatedAt\n */\nexport interface UserRecord {\n  userId: string;\n  email: string;\n  passwordHash: string;\n  passwordSalt: string;\n  createdAt: number;\n  updatedAt: number;\n}\n\nconst users = new Map<string, UserRecord>();\n\n/**\n * Find user by email.\n */\nexport function findUserByEmail(email: string): UserRecord | undefined {\n  return Array.from(users.values()).find((u) => u.email.toLowerCase() === email.toLowerCase());\n}\n\n/**\n * Find user by user ID.\n */\nexport function users.set(user.userId, user);\n}\n\n/**\n * Delete a user by ID.\n * Used for test cleanup.\n */\nexport function deleteUser(userId: string): boolean {\n  return users.delete(userId);\n}\n\n/**\n * ============================================================================\n\n/**\n * Get password policy requirements.\n *\n * Returns the current password policy including length requirements,\n * complexity requirements, and other security settings.\n */\nexport const getPasswordPolicyHandler: MiddlewareHandler = async (c) => {\n  const policy = getPasswordPolicyDescription();\n\n  return c.json({\n    policy,\n    requirements: {\n      minLength: policy.minLength,\n      maxLength: policy.maxLength,\n      requireUppercase: policy.requireUppercase,\n      requireLowercase: policy.requireLowercase,\n      requireNumbers: policy.requireNumbers,\n      requireSpecialChars: policy.requireSpecialChars,\n      allowSpaces: policy.allowSpaces,\n      expirationDays: policy.expirationDays,\n      historyCount: policy.historyCount,\n    },\n    tips: [\n      \"Use at least 12 characters\",\n      \"Include uppercase and lowercase letters\",\n      \"Add numbers and special characters\",\n      \"Avoid common words or patterns\",\n      \"Don't reuse recent passwords\",\n    ],\n  });\n};\n\n/**\n * Request password reset.\n *\n * Initiates the password reset flow by:\n * 1. Validating the email address\n * 2. Checking if account is locked (too many failed attempts)\n * 3. Rate limiting (strict tier: 5 requests/minute)\n * 4. Checking if user exists (but not revealing this)\n * 5. Generating a secure reset token with device fingerprinting\n * 6. Sending email with reset link\n * 7. Invalidating any existing reset tokens\n */\nexport const requestPasswordResetHandler: MiddlewareHandler = async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const body = await c.req.json().catch(() => ({}));\n    const validationResult = passwordResetRequestSchema.safeParse(body);\n\n    if (!validationResult.success) {\n      return c.json(\n        {\n          error: \"Invalid request\",\n          details: validationResult.error.errors,\n        },\n        400\n      );\n    }\n\n    const { email } = validationResult.data;\n\n    // Get client IP and user agent for rate limiting and security logging\n    const clientIp =\n      c.req.header(\"CF-Connecting-IP\") ||\n      c.req.header(\"X-Forwarded-For\")?.split(\",\")[0]?.trim() ||\n      c.req.header(\"X-Real-IP\") ||\n      \"unknown\";\n    const userAgent = c.req.header(\"User-Agent\");\n\n    // Check if account is locked (prevent enumeration - same response)\n    const lockStatus = isAccountLocked(email);\n    if (lockStatus.locked) {\n      // Return same response as success to prevent enumeration\n      // But log internally for monitoring\n      logger.warn(\"Password reset request blocked - account locked\", {\n        email,\n        clientIp,\n        remainingMinutes: lockStatus.remainingMinutes,\n      });\n\n      return c.json({\n        success: true,\n        message: \"If an account exists with this email, a password reset link has been sent.\",\n      });\n    }\n\n    // Check if user exists\n    const user = findUserByEmail(email);\n\n    // Always return success to prevent email enumeration\n    // invalidateResetTokensForKey(user.userId);\n\n      // Generate new reset token with device fingerprinting\n      const resetData = await generatePasswordResetToken(user.userId, clientIp, userAgent);\n\n      // Send password reset email\n      const emailResult = await sendPasswordResetEmail({\n        email,\n        tokenId: resetData.tokenId,\n        token: resetData.token,\n        expiresAt: resetData.expiresAt,\n        clientIp,\n      });\n\n      if (emailResult.success) {\n        logger.info(\"Password reset email sent\", {\n          userId: user.userId,\n          email,\n          clientIp,\n          deviceInfo: resetData.deviceInfo,\n          messageId: emailResult.messageId,\n        });\n      } else {\n        logger.error(\"Failed to send password reset email\", {\n          userId: user.userId,\n          email,\n          error: emailResult.error,\n        });\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Always return success (prevent email enumeration)\n    return c.json({\n      success: true,\n      message: \"If an account exists with this email, a password reset link has been sent.\",\n    });\n  } catch (error) {\n    logger.error(\"Password reset request failed\", error as Error);\n\n    return c.json(\n      {\n        error: \"Failed to process password reset request\",\n        message: error instanceof Error ? error.message : \"Unknown error\",\n      },\n      500\n    );\n  }\n};\n\n/**\n * Confirm password reset.\n *\n * Completes the password reset flow by:\n * 1. Validating the reset token with device verification\n * 2. Recording failed attempts and checking account lockout\n * 3. Validating the new password against policy\n * 4. Updating the user's password\n * 5. Consuming the reset token (single-use)\n * 6. Invalidating all other reset tokens\n * 7. Invalidating all existing sessions (force re-login)\n * 8. Clearing failed attempts on success\n * 9. Sending security notification email\n */\nexport const confirmPasswordResetHandler: MiddlewareHandler = async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const body = await c.req.json().catch(() => ({}));\n    const validationResult = passwordResetConfirmSchema.safeParse(body);\n\n    if (!validationResult.success) {\n      return c.json(\n        {\n          error: \"Invalid request\",\n          details: validationResult.error.errors,\n        },\n        400\n      );\n    }\n\n    const { tokenId, token, newPassword } = validationResult.data;\n\n    const clientIp =\n      c.req.header(\"CF-Connecting-IP\") ||\n      c.req.header(\"X-Forwarded-For\")?.split(\",\")[0]?.trim() ||\n      c.req.header(\"X-Real-IP\") ||\n      \"unknown\";\n    const userAgent = c.req.header(\"User-Agent\");\n\n    // Validate the reset token with device verification\n    const validationResult_ = await validatePasswordResetToken(tokenId, token, clientIp, userAgent);\n\n    if (!validationResult_.keyId) {\n      // Record failed attempt\n      securityLogger.logSuspiciousActivity(c, \"invalid_password_reset_token\");\n\n      // Try to get user email from token for attempt tracking\n      const tokenData = (await import(\"../middleware/password-management.js\"))\n        ._getPasswordResetTokensMap()\n        .get(tokenId);\n      if (tokenData) {\n        const user = getUserById(tokenData.keyId);\n        if (user) {\n          const attemptResult = recordFailedResetAttempt(user.email, clientIp);\n          if (attemptResult.locked) {\n            logger.warn(\"Account locked after too many failed reset attempts\", {\n              email: user.email,\n              clientIp,\n              attempts: attemptResult.attemptCount,\n            });\n          }\n        }\n      }\n\n      return c.json(\n        {\n          error: \"Invalid or expired reset token\",\n          message: \"The reset link is invalid or has expired. Please request a new password reset.\",\n        },\n        400\n      );\n    }\n\n    const keyId = validationResult_.keyId;\n\n    // Get the user\n    const user = getUserById(keyId);\n\n    if (!user) {\n      return c.json(\n        {\n          error: \"User not found\",\n          message: \"The account associated with this reset link no longer exists.\",\n        },\n        404\n      );\n    }\n\n    // Check if account is locked\n    const lockStatus = isAccountLocked(user.email);\n    if (lockStatus.locked) {\n      return c.json(\n        {\n          error: \"Account temporarily locked\",\n          message: `Too many failed password reset attempts. Please try again in ${lockStatus.remainingMinutes} minutes.`,\n        },\n        429\n      );\n    }\n\n    // Validate the new password against policy\n    const passwordValidation = await validatePassword(newPassword, {}, keyId);\n\n    if (!passwordValidation.valid) {\n      return c.json(\n        {\n          error: \"Password does not meet security requirements\",\n          errors: passwordValidation.errors,\n        },\n        400\n      );\n    }\n\n    // Store old password in history before changing\n    storePasswordInHistory(keyId, user.passwordHash, user.passwordSalt);\n\n    // Hash the new password\n    const passwordHash = await hashPassword(newPassword);\n\n    // Update user password\n    user.passwordHash = passwordHash.hash;\n    user.passwordSalt = passwordHash.salt;\n    user.updatedAt = Date.now();\n    upsertUser(user);\n\n    // Consume the reset token (single-use)\n    consumePasswordResetToken(tokenId);\n\n    // Invalidate all other reset tokens for this user\n    invalidateResetTokensForKey(keyId);\n\n    // Invalidate all existing sessions for this user (force re-login)\n    const sessionsInvalidated = invalidateAllSessionsForKey(keyId);\n\n    // Clear failed reset attempts on successful reset\n    clearFailedResetAttempts(user.email);\n\n    // Send security notification email\n    const deviceInfo = getDeviceInfo(userAgent);\n    const notificationResult = await sendPasswordResetNotificationEmail({\n      email: user.email,\n      clientIp,\n      deviceInfo,\n    });\n\n    logger.info(\"Password reset completed\", {\n      userId: keyId,\n      email: user.email,\n      clientIp,\n      deviceInfo,\n      sessionsInvalidated,\n      notificationSent: notificationResult.success,\n    });\n\n    const responsePayload: {\n      success: boolean;\n      message: string;\n      warning?: string;\n    } = {\n      success: true,\n      message: \"Password has been reset successfully. Please log in with your new password.\",\n    };\n\n    // Add warning if device changed\n    if (validationResult_.deviceChanged && validationResult_.warning) {\n      responsePayload.warning = validationResult_.warning;\n    }\n\n    return c.json(responsePayload);\n  } catch (error) {\n    logger.error(\"Password reset confirmation failed\", error as Error);\n\n    return c.json(\n      {\n        error: \"Failed to reset password\",\n        message: error instanceof Error ? error.message : \"Unknown error\",\n      },\n      500\n    );\n  }\n};\n\n/**\n * Change password for authenticated user.\n *\n * Allows authenticated users to change their password by:\n * 1. Verifying their current password\n * 2. Validating the new password against policy\n * 3. Updating the password\n * 4. Logging the change for audit\n */\nexport const changePasswordHandler: MiddlewareHandler = async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const auth = getRbacAuthContext(c);\n\n    if (!auth) {\n      return c.json({ error: \"Authentication required\" }, 401);\n    }\n\n    const body = await c.req.json().catch(() => ({}));\n    const validationResult = passwordChangeSchema.safeParse(body);\n\n    if (!validationResult.success) {\n      return c.json(\n        {\n          error: \"Invalid request\",\n          details: validationResult.error.errors,\n        },\n        400\n      );\n    }\n\n    const { currentPassword, newPassword } = validationResult.data;\n\n    // Get the user\n    const user = getUserById(auth.keyId);\n\n    if (!user) {\n      return c.json({ error: \"User not found\" }, 404);\n    }\n\n    // Verify current password\n    const currentPasswordValid = await verifyPasswordHash(\n      currentPassword,\n      user.passwordHash,\n      user.passwordSalt\n    );\n\n    if (!currentPasswordValid) {\n      securityLogger.logAuthFailure(c, \"invalid_current_password\");\n      return c.json(\n        {\n          error: \"Current password is incorrect\",\n          message: \"The current password you provided is incorrect. Please try again.\",\n        },\n        400\n      );\n    }\n\n    // Validate the new password against policy\n    const passwordValidation = await validatePassword(newPassword, {}, auth.keyId);\n\n    if (!passwordValidation.valid) {\n      return c.json(\n        {\n          error: \"Password does not meet security requirements\",\n          errors: passwordValidation.errors,\n        },\n        400\n      );\n    }\n\n    // Hash the new password\n    const passwordHashData = await hashPassword(newPassword);\n\n    // Update user password\n    user.passwordHash = passwordHashData.hash;\n    user.passwordSalt = passwordHashData.salt;\n    user.updatedAt = Date.now();\n    upsertUser(user);\n\n    logger.info(\"Password changed\", { userId: auth.keyId });\n\n    return c.json({\n      success: true,\n      message: \"Password has been changed successfully.\",\n    });\n  } catch (error) {\n    logger.error(\"Password change failed\", error as Error);\n\n    return c.json(\n      {\n        error: \"Failed to change password\",\n        message: error instanceof Error ? error.message : \"Unknown error\",\n      },\n      500\n    );\n  }\n};\n\n// ============================================================================\n// Route Builder\n// ============================================================================\n\n/**\n * Build password reset routes with all middleware.\n */\nexport function buildPasswordResetRoutes() {\n  const handlers = {\n    getPasswordPolicy: getPasswordPolicyHandler,\n    requestPasswordReset: [\n      // Apply strict rate limiting (5 requests per minute)\n      authRateLimit(\"strict\", { addHeaders: true }),\n      // Require CAPTCHA after rate limit violations\n      requireCaptcha({ alwaysRequired: false }),\n      auditLogAccess(\"password\", \"reset_request\"),\n      requestPasswordResetHandler,\n    ],\n    confirmPasswordReset: [\n      // Apply strict rate limiting\n      authRateLimit(\"strict\", { addHeaders: true }),\n      // Require CAPTCHA after rate limit violations\n      requireCaptcha({ alwaysRequired: false }),\n      auditLogAccess(\"password\", \"reset_confirm\"),\n      confirmPasswordResetHandler,\n    ],\n    changePassword: [\n      requireResourceAccess(\"password\", \"update\"),\n      auditLogAccess(\"password\", \"change\"),\n      changePasswordHandler,\n    ],\n  };\n\n  return handlers;\n}\n","numLines":597,"startLine":1,"totalLines":597}}}

void {\n435\t  // Allow empty string to disable pepper\n436\t  if (pepper === \"\") {\n437\t    PASSWORD_PEPPER = \"\";\n438\t    logger.info(\"Password pepper disabled\");\n439\t    return;\n440\t  }\n441\t\n442\t  // Validate pepper is a valid hex string\n443\t  if (!/^[a-fA-F0-9]+$/.test(pepper)) {\n444\t    throw new Error(\"Password pepper must be a hex string\");\n445\t  }\n446\t  if getPasswordPepper(): string {\n460\t  return PASSWORD_PEPPER;\n461\t}\n462\t\n463\t// ============================================================================\n464\t// Password Reset Attempt Tracking & Account Lockout\n465\t// ============================================================================\n466\t\n467\t/**\n468\t * Check if an account is currently locked due to too many failed reset attempts.\n469\t *\n470\t * @param email - The email address to check\n471\t * @returns Object indicating if locked and when it will be unlocked\n472\t */\n473\texport function isAccountLocked(email: string): {\n474\t  locked: boolean;\n475\t  reason?: string;\n476\t  unlockTime?: number;\n477\t  remainingMinutes?: number;\n478\t} {\n479\t  const normalizedEmail = };\n491\t  }\n492\t\n493\t  const remainingMinutes = Math.ceil((lockout.lockedUntil - Date.now()) / (60 * 1000));\n494\t\n495\t  return {\n496\t    locked: true,\n497\t    reason: is now locked and details\n510\t */\n511\texport function recordFailedResetAttempt(\n512\t  email: string,\n513\t  clientIp: string\n514\t): {\n515\t  locked: boolean;\n516\t  attemptCount: number;\n517\t  remainingAttempts: number;\n518\t  lockedUntil?: number;\n519\t} {\n520\t  const normalizedEmail = email.toLowerCase();\n521\t  const key = `${normalizedEmail}:${clientIp}`;\n522\t  const now = Date.now();\n523\t\n524\t  let attempt = passwordResetAttempts.get(key);\n525\t\n526\t  // Reset if window has expired\n527\t  if (!attempt || now > attempt.resetAt) {\n528\t    attempt = { count: 0, resetAt: now + RESET_ATTEMPT_WINDOW_MS };\n529\t  }\n530\t\n531\t  attempt.count++;\n532\t  passwordResetAttempts.set(key, attempt);\n533\t\n534\t  // Also track IP-agnostic attempts (same email from any IP)\n535\t  let globalAttempt = passwordResetAttempts.get(normalizedEmail);\n536\t  if (!globalAttempt || now > globalAttempt.resetAt) {\n537\t    globalAttempt = { count: 0, resetAt: now + RESET_ATTEMPT_WINDOW_MS };\n538\t  }\n539\t  globalAttempt.count++;\n540\t  passwordResetAttempts.set(normalizedEmail, globalAttempt);\n541\t\n542\t  const remainingAttempts = Math.max(0, globalAttempt.count,\n551\t    });\n552\t\n553\t    logger.warn(\"Account locked due to too many failed reset attempts\", {\n554\t      email: normalizedEmail,\n555\t      clientIp,\n556\t      attempts: globalAttempt.count,\n557\t      lockedUntil: new Date(lockedUntil).toISOString(),\n558\t    });\n559\t\n560\t    return {\n561\t      locked: true,\n562\t      attemptCount: globalAttempt.count,\n563\t      remainingAttempts: 0,\n564\t      lockedUntil,\n565\t    };\n566\t  }\n567\t\n568\t  return {\n569\t    locked: false,\n570\t    attemptCount: globalAttempt.count,\n571\t    remainingAttempts,\n572\t  };\n573\t}\n574\t\n575\t/**\n576\t * Clear failed reset attempts for an email (e.g., after successful reset).\n577\t *\n578\t * @param email - The email address\n579\t */\n580\texport function clearFailedResetAttempts(email: string): void {\n581\t  const normalizedEmail = email.toLowerCase();\n582\t\n583\t  // Remove all entries that start with this email\n584\t  for (const key of passwordResetAttempts.keys()) {\n585\t    if (key === normalizedEmail || key.startsWith(`${normalizedEmail}:`)) {\n586\t      passwordResetAttempts.delete(key);\n587\t    }\n588\t  }\n589\t\n590\t  // Also remove from lockouts\n591\t  accountLockouts.delete(normalizedEmail);\n592\t}\n593\t\n594\t/**\n595\t * Get current attempts\n600\t */\n601\texport function getFailedResetAttemptCount(email: string, clientIp: string): number {\n602\t  const normalizedEmail = email.toLowerCase();\n603\t  const key = `${normalizedEmail}:${clientIp}`;\n604\t  const attempt = passwordResetAttempts.get(key);\n605\t\n606\t  if (!attempt || Date.now() > attempt.resetAt) {\n607\t    return 0;\n608\t  }\n609\t\n610\t @internal\n618\t */\n619\texport function _startTokenCleanup(): void {\n620\t  if (tokenCleanupInterval) {\n621\t    return; // Already running\n622\t  }\n623\t\n624\t  tokenCleanupInterval = setInterval(() => {\n625\t    const now = Date.now();\n626\t    let cleaned = 0;\n627\t\n628\t    for (const [tokenId, tokenData] of passwordResetTokens.entries()) {\n629\t      // Remove expired or used tokens\n630\t      if (now > tokenData.expiresAt || tokenData.used) {\n631\t        passwordResetTokens.delete(tokenId);\n632\t        cleaned++;\n633\t      }\n634\t    }\n635\t\n636\t    // Clean expired lockouts\n637\t    for (const [email, lockout] of accountLockouts.entries()) {\n638\t      if (now > lockout.lockedUntil) {\n639\t        accountLockouts.delete(email);\n640\t        passwordResetAttempts.delete(email);\n641\t      }\n642\t    }\n643\t\n644\t    if (cleaned > 0) {\n645\t      logger.debug(\"Token cleanup completed\", { cleaned, remaining: passwordResetTokens.size });\n646\t    }\n647\t  }, TOKEN_CLEANUP_INTERVAL_MS);\n648\t\n649\t  logger.info(\"Token cleanup interval started\", { intervalMs: TOKEN_CLEANUP_INTERVAL_MS });\n650\t}\n651\t\n652\t/**\n653\t * Stop the automatic token cleanup interval.\n654\t *\n655\t * @internal\n656\t */\n657\texport function _stopTokenCleanup(): void {\n658\t  if (tokenCleanupInterval) {\n659\t    clearInterval(tokenCleanupInterval);\n660\t    tokenCleanupInterval = null;\n661\t    logger.info(\"Token cleanup interval stopped\");\n662\t  }\n663\t}\n664\t\n665\t/**\n666\t * Manually trigger token cleanup.\n667\t * Useful for testing or immediate cleanup.\n668\t *\n669\t * @returns Number of tokens cleaned up\n670\t */\n671\texport function cleanupExpiredTokens(): number {\n672\t  const now = Date.now();\n673\t  let cleaned = 0;\n674\t\n675\t  for (const [tokenId, tokenData] of passwordResetTokens.entries()) {\n676\t    if (now > tokenData.expiresAt || tokenData.used) {\n677\t      passwordResetTokens.delete(tokenId);\n678\t      cleaned++;\n679\t    }\n680\t  }\n681\t\n682\t  // Clean expired lockouts\n683\t  for (const [email, lockout] of accountLockouts.entries()) {\n684\t    if (now > lockout.lockedUntil) {\n685\t      accountLockouts.delete(email);\n686\t      passwordResetAttempts.delete(email);\n687\t    }\n688\t  }\n689\t\n690\t  return cleaned;\n691\t}\n692\t\n693\t// ============================================================================\n694\t// Password Validation\n695\t// ============================================================================\n696\t\n697\t/**\n698\t * Detect sequential character patterns in password.\n699\t * Checks for:\n700\t * - Numeric sequences: 1234, 4321, 0123\n701\t * - Alphabetic sequences: abcd, DCBA, mnop\n702\t * - Both forward and reverse sequences\n703\t *\n704\t * @param password - The password to check\n705\t * @param maxSequence - Maximum allowed sequential characters\n706\t * @returns Object indicating if sequential pattern was found and the pattern\n707\t */\n708\tfunction detectSequentialChars(\n709\t  password: string,\n710\t  maxSequence: number\n711\t): { found: boolean; pattern?: string } {\n712\t  const lowerPassword = password.toLowerCase();\n713\t\n714\t  // Check each position for sequences\n715\t  for (let i = 0; i < lowerPassword.length - (maxSequence - 1); i++) {\n716\t    // Extract potential sequence\n717\t    const sequence = lowerPassword.substring(i, i + maxSequence + 1);\n718\t\n719\t    // Check if it's a valid sequence (all letters or all digits)\n720\t    const isAllLetters = /^[a-z]+$/.test(sequence);\n721\t    const isAllDigits = /^\\d+$/.test(sequence);\n722\t\n723\t    if (!isAllLetters && !isAllDigits) {\n724\t      continue;\n725\t    }\n726\t\n727\t    // Check for forward or reverse sequential pattern\n728\t    if (isSequentialSequence(sequence)) {\n729\t      return { found: true, pattern: sequence };\n730\t    }\n731\t  }\n732\t\n733\t  return { found: false };\n734\t}\n735\t\n736\t/**\n737\t * Check if a string is a sequential character pattern.\n738\t * Handles both forward (abcd, 1234) and reverse (dcba, 4321) sequences.\n739\t */\n740\tfunction isSequentialSequence(str: string): boolean {\n741\t  if (str.length < 2) return false;\n742\t\n743\t  // Check forward sequence\n744\t  let isForward = true;\n745\t  let isReverse = true;\n746\t\n747\t  for (let i = 0; i < str.length - 1; i++) {\n748\t    const current = str.charCodeAt(i);\n749\t    const next = str.charCodeAt(i + 1);\n750\t\n751\t    // Forward: next char is exactly +1\n752\t    if (next !== current + 1) {\n753\t      isForward = false;\n754\t    }\n755\t\n756\t    // Reverse: next char is exactly -1\n757\t    if (next !== current - 1) {\n758\t      isReverse = false;\n759\t    }\n760\t  }\n761\t\n762\t  return isForward || isReverse;\n763\t}\n764\t\n765\t/**\n766\t * Detect keyboard walking patterns in password.\n767\t * Checks for common keyboard sequences like \"qwerty\", \"asdf\", \"1qaz\", etc.\n768\t *\n769\t * Only reports patterns of 3+ characters to avoid false positives on\n770\t * single characters that happen to be part of keyboard layouts.\n771\t *\n772\t * @param password - The password to check\n773\t * @returns Object indicating if keyboard pattern was found and the pattern\n774\t */\n775\tfunction detectKeyboardPatterns(password: string): { found: boolean; pattern?: string } {\n776\t  const lowerPassword = password.toLowerCase();\n777\t  const MIN_PATTERN_LENGTH = 3;\n778\t\n779\t  // Check each pattern\n780\t  for (const pattern of KEYBOARD_PATTERNS) {\n781\t    // Skip patterns shorter than minimum length\n782\t    if (pattern.length < MIN_PATTERN_LENGTH) {\n783\t      continue;\n784\t    }\n785\t\n786\t    // Check if pattern exists in password (case-insensitive)\n787\t    if (lowerPassword.includes(pattern)) {\n788\t      return { found: true, pattern };\n789\t    }\n790\t\n791\t    // Also check reversed version of pattern\n792\t    const reversed = pattern.split(\"\").reverse().join(\"\");\n793\t    if (lowerPassword.includes(reversed)) {\n794\t      return { found: true, pattern: reversed };\n795\t    }\n796\t  }\n797\t\n798\t  return { found: false };\n799\t}\n800\t\n801\t/**\n802\t * Detect common password variations like \"password1\", \"password2\", etc.\n803\t *\n804\t * @param password - The password to check\n805\t * @param skipKeyboardBased - Whether to skip keyboard-based common words (when blockKeyboardPatterns is false)\n806\t * @returns Object indicating if common variation was found\n807\t */\n808\tfunction detectCommonVariations(\n809\t  password: string,\n810\t  skipKeyboardBased = false\n811\t): { found: boolean; pattern?: string } {\n812\t  const lowerPassword = password.toLowerCase();\n813\t\n814\t  // Common base passwords with number/special char variations\n815\t  // Keyboard-based words (qwerty, asdf) are skipped when blockKeyboardPatterns is false\n816\t  const commonBases = [\n817\t    \"password\",\n818\t    \"passw0rd\",\n819\t    \"admin\",\n820\t    \"welcome\",\n821\t    \"login\",\n822\t    // Skip keyboard-based words when requested\n823\t    ...(skipKeyboardBased ? [] : [\"qwerty\"]),\n824\t    \"letmein\",\n825\t    \"monkey\",\n826\t    \"dragon\",\n827\t    \"master\",\n828\t  ];\n829\t\n830\t  for (const base of commonBases) {\n831\t    // Check if password starts with common base\n832\t    if (!lowerPassword.startsWith(base)) {\n833\t      continue;\n834\t    }\n835\t\n836\t    const suffix = lowerPassword.slice(base.length);\n837\t\n838\t    // If there's no suffix, it's just the base word (handled elsewhere)\n839\t    if (suffix.length === 0) {\n840\t      continue;\n841\t    }\n842\t\n843\t    // Check if suffix is only numbers\n844\t    if (/^\\d+$/.test(suffix)) {\n845\t      return { found: true, pattern: base + \"[numbers]\" };\n846\t    }\n847\t\n848\t    // Check if suffix is only special characters\n849\t    if (/^[!@#$%^&*]+$/.test(suffix)) {\n850\t      return { found: true, pattern: base + \"[special]\" };\n851\t    }\n852\t\n853\t    // Check if suffix is a year (19xx or 20xx)\n854\t    if (/^(19\\d\\d|20\\d\\d)$/.test(suffix)) {\n855\t      return { found: true, pattern: base + \"[year]\" };\n856\t    }\n857\t\n858\t    // Check if suffix is numbers followed by special chars (e.g., \"password123!@#\")\n859\t    if (/^\\d+[!@#$%^&*]+$/.test(suffix)) {\n860\t      return { found: true, pattern: base + \"[numbers+special]\" };\n861\t    }\n862\t\n863\t    // Check if suffix is special chars followed by numbers (e.g., \"password!@#123\")\n864\t    if (/^[!@#$%^&*]+\\d+$/.test(suffix)) {\n865\t      return { found: true, pattern: base + \"[special+numbers]\" };\n866\t    }\n867\t\n868\t    // Check if suffix is a year followed by special chars (e.g., \"password2024!@#\")\n869\t    if (/^(19\\d\\d|20\\d\\d)[!@#$%^&*]+$/.test(suffix)) {\n870\t      return { found: true, pattern: base + \"[year+special]\" };\n871\t    }\n872\t  }\n873\t\n874\t  return { found: false };\n875\t}\n876\t\n877\t/**\n878\t * Validate a password against policy requirements.\n879\t *\n880\t * Optional custom policy (uses defaults if not provided)\n890\t * @param keyId - Optional key ID for password history checking\n891\t * @returns Validation result with detailed feedback\n892\t */\n893\texport async function validatePassword(\n894\t  password: string,\n895\t  policy: PasswordPolicy = {},\n896\t  keyId?: string\n897\t): Promise<PasswordValidationResult> {\n898\t  const mergedPolicy = { ...DEFAULT_PASSWORD_POLICY, ...policy };\n899\t  const errors: string[] = [];\n900\t\n901\t  // Check maximum length FIRST before any sanitization\n902\t  // This ensures we catch long passwords and provide a clear error message\n903\t  if (password.length > mergedPolicy.maxLength) {\n904\t    errors.push(`Password must be no more than ${mergedPolicy.maxLength} characters long`);\n905\t    return {\n906\t      valid: false,\n907\t      errors,\n908\t      strength: 0,\n909\t      strengthCategory: \"weak\",\n910\t    };\n911\t  }\n912\t\n913\t  // Check minimum length\n914\t  if (password.length < mergedPolicy.minLength) {\n915\t    errors.push(`Password must be at least ${mergedPolicy.minLength} characters long`);\n916\t  }\n917\t\n918\t  // Sanitize input to prevent injection attacks (without length truncation since we already checked)\n919\t  // For passwords, we only do basic sanitization - no SQL/Command injection prevention\n920\t  // since those would incorrectly reject valid passwords containing words like \"or\", \"and\", etc.\n921\t  const sanitizedPassword = sanitizeStringSimple(password, {\n922\t    maxLength: password.length, // Don't truncate, we already validated length\n923\t    preserveCase: true,\n924\t    preserveWhitespace: mergedPolicy.allowSpaces,\n925\t    preventSqlInjection: false, // Don't prevent SQL injection in passwords\n926\t    preventCommandInjection: false, // Don't prevent command injection in passwords\n927\t    preventLdapInjection: false, // Don't prevent LDAP injection in passwords\n928\t    preventNosqlInjection: false, // Don't prevent NoSQL injection in passwords\n929\t  });\n930\t\n931\t  // Check if sanitization changed the password (injection patterns detected)\n932\t  // We only check for XSS patterns in passwords since those are actual security risks\n933\t  if (sanitizedPassword !== password) {\n934\t    errors.push(\"Password contains invalid characters\");\n935\t    return {\n936\t      valid: false,\n937\t      errors,\n938\t      strength: 0,\n939\t      strengthCategory: \"weak\",\n940\t    };\n941\t  }\n942\t\n943\t  // Check uppercase\n944\t  if (mergedPolicy.requireUppercase && !/[A-Z]/.test(password)) {\n945\t    errors.push(\"Password must contain at least one uppercase letter\");\n946\t  }\n947\t\n948\t  // Check lowercase\n949\t  if (mergedPolicy.requireLowercase && !/[a-z]/.test(password)) {\n950\t    errors.push(\"Password must contain at least one lowercase letter\");\n951\t  }\n952\t\n953\t  // Check numbers\n954\t  if (mergedPolicy.requireNumbers && !/\\d/.test(password)) {\n955\t    errors.push(\"Password must contain at least one number\");\n956\t  }\n957\t\n958\t  // Check special characters\n959\t  if (mergedPolicy.requireSpecialChars && !/[!@#$%^&*()_+\\-=[\\]{};':\"\\\\|,.<>/?]/.test(password)) {\n960\t    errors.push(\"Password must contain at least one special character\");\n961\t  }\n962\t\n963\t  // Check spaces\n964\t  if (!mergedPolicy.allowSpaces && /\\s/.test(password)) {\n965\t    errors.push(\"Password cannot contain spaces\");\n966\t  }\n967\t\n968\t  // Check against blocked passwords (exact match only)\n969\t  // Substring matching is too aggressive and would reject valid passwords\n970\t  // like \"SecurePass123!\" that happen to contain common words\n971\t  const lowerPassword = password.toLowerCase();\n972\t  for (const blocked of mergedPolicy.blockedPasswords) {\n973\t    if (lowerPassword === blocked) {\n974\t      errors.push(\"Password is too common or weak\");\n975\t      break;\n976\t    }\n977\t  }\n978\t\n979\t  // Check character repetition\n980\t  if (mergedPolicy.maxRepetition > 0) {\n981\t    const repetitionRegex = new RegExp(`(.)\\\\1{${mergedPolicy.maxRepetition},}`, \"g\");\n982\t    if (repetitionRegex.test(password)) {\n983\t      errors.push(\n984\t        `Password cannot contain the same character more than ${mergedPolicy.maxRepetition} times in a row`\n985\t      );\n986\t    }\n987\t  }\n988\t\n989\t  // Check sequential character patterns\n990\t  if (mergedPolicy.blockSequentialChars && mergedPolicy.maxSequentialChars > 0) {\n991\t    const sequentialResult = detectSequentialChars(password, mergedPolicy.maxSequentialChars);\n992\t    if (sequentialResult.found) {\n993\t      errors.push(\n994\t        `Password contains sequential characters (${sequentialResult.pattern}). Avoid using patterns like \"1234\" or \"abcd\".`\n995\t      );\n996\t    }\n997\t  }\n998\t\n999\t  // Check keyboard walking patterns\n1000\t  if (mergedPolicy.blockKeyboardPatterns) {\n1001\t    const keyboardResult = detectKeyboardPatterns(password);\n1002\t    if (keyboardResult.found) {\n1003\t      errors.push(\n1004\t        `Password contains keyboard pattern (${keyboardResult.pattern}). Please choose a more unique password.`\n1015\t    );\n1016\t  }\n1017\t\n1018\t  // Calculate strength score\n1019\t  const strength = calculatePasswordStrength(password);\n1020\t  const strengthCategory = getStrengthCategory(strength);\n1021\t\n1022\t  // Check password history if keyId provided\n1023\t  if (keyId && mergedPolicy.passwordHistoryCount > 0) {\n1024\t    const history = passwordHistory.get(keyId);\n1025\t    if (history) {\n1026\t      // Check against recent passwords\n1027\t      const recentHistory = history.slice(-mergedPolicy.passwordHistoryCount);\n1028\t      for (const entry of recentHistory) {\n1029\t        if (await verifyPasswordHash(password, entry.hash, entry.salt)) {\n1030\t          errors.push(\"Cannot reuse a recent password\");\n1031\t          break;\n1032\t        }\n1033\t      }\n1034\t    }\n1035\t  }\n1036\t\n1037\t  // Check breached passwords via HIBP API\n1038\t  let breached = false;\n1039\t  let breachCount = 0;\n1040\t  if (mergedPolicy.checkBreachedPasswords && errors.length === 0) {\n1041\t    const breachResult = await checkBreachedPassword(password);\n1042\t    breached = breachResult.breached;\n1043\t    breachCount = breachResult.count;\n1044\t\n1045\t    if (breached && breachCount > (mergedPolicy.maxBreachedCount ?? 0)) {\n1046\t      errors.push(\n1047\t        `This password has been found in data breaches ${breachCount} times. Please choose a different password.`\n1048\t      );\n1049\t    }\n1050\t  }\n1051\t\n1052\t  // Check minimum strength score\n1053\t  if (strength < (mergedPolicy.minStrengthScore ?? 0)) {\n1054\t    errors.push(\n1055\t      `Password is too weak (strength: ${strength}/100). Please choose a stronger password.`\n1056\t    );\n1057\t  }\n1058\t\n1059\t  return {\n1060\t    valid: errors.length === 0,\n1061\t    errors,\n1062\t    strength,\n1063\t    strengthCategory,\n1064\t    breached,\n1065\t    breachCount: breached ? breachCount : undefined,\n1066\t  };\n1067\t}\n1068\t\n1069\t/**\n1070\t * Calculate password strength score (0-100).\n1071\t *\n1072\t * Uses entropy-based calculation with bonuses for:\n1073\t * - Length\n1074\t * - Character variety\n1075\t * - Character distribution\n1076\t */\n1077\tfunction calculatePasswordStrength(password: string): number {\n1078\t  let score = 0;\n1079\t\n1080\t  // Length score (up to 40 points)\n1081\t  score += Math.min(40, password.length * 2);\n1082\t\n1083\t  // Character variety (up to 30 points)\n1084\t  if (/[a-z]/.test(password)) score += 5;\n1085\t  if (/[A-Z]/.test(password)) score += 5;\n1086\t  if (/\\d/.test(password)) score += 5;\n1087\t  if (/[!@#$%^&*()_+\\-=[\\]{};':\"\\\\|,.<>/?]/.test(password)) score += 10;\n1088\t  if (/\\s/.test(password)) score += 5;\n1089\t\n1090\t  // Character distribution (up to 20 points)\n1091\t  const uniqueChars = new Set(password).size;\n1092\t  score += Math.min(20, (uniqueChars / password.length) * 20);\n1093\t\n1094\t  // Complexity bonus (up to 10 points)\n1095\t  const hasMixedCase = /[a-z]/.test(password) && /[A-Z]/.test(password);\n1096\t  const hasNumbers = /\\d/.test(password);\n1097\t  const hasSpecial = /[!@#$%^&*()_+\\-=\\[\\]{};':\"\\\\|,.<>\\/?]/.test(password);\n1098\t  if (hasMixedCase && hasNumbers && hasSpecial) score += 10;\n1099\t\n1100\t  return Math.min(100, score);\n1101\t}\n1102\t\n1103\t/**\n1104\t * Get strength category from score.\n1105\t */\n1106\tfunction getStrengthCategory(score: number): \"weak\" | \"fair\" | \"good\" | \"strong\" {\n1107\t  if (score < 40) return \"weak\";\n1108\t  if (score < 60) return \"fair\";\n1109\t  if (score < 80) return \"good\";\n1110\t  return \"strong\";\n1111\t}\n1112\t\n1113\t/**\n1114\t * Check if a password has been breached using Have I Been Pwned k-anonymity API.\n1115\t *\n1116\t * Uses the k-anonymity model where only the first 5 characters of the\n1117\t * SHA-256 hash are sent to the API. The full hash never leaves the server.\n1118\t *\n1119\t * Results are cached for 1 hour to reduce API calls and improve performance.\n1120\t *\n1121\t * @param password - The password to check\n1122\t * @returns Object indicating if breached and the count\n1123\t */\n1124\tasync function checkBreachedPassword(\n1125\t  password: string\n1126\t): Promise<{ breached: boolean; count: number }> {\n1127\t  try {\n1128\t    // Calculate SHA-256 hash of password\n1129\t    const encoder = new TextEncoder();\n1130\t    const data = encoder.encode(password);\n1131\t    const hashBuffer = await crypto.subtle.digest(\"SHA-256\", data);\n1132\t    const hashArray = Array.from(new Uint8Array(hashBuffer));\n1133\t    const hash = hashArray.map((b) => b.toString(16).padStart(2, \"0\")).join(\"\");\n1134\t\n1135\t    // Get first 5 characters for API request (cache key)\n1136\t    const prefix = hash.substring(0, 5);\n1137\t    const suffix = hash.substring(5);\n1138\t\n1139\t    // Check cache first\n1140\t    const cached = breachedPasswordCache.get(prefix);\n1141\t    const now = Date.now();\n1142\t    if (cached && now < cached.expiresAt) {\n1143\t      // Check if our specific suffix matches\n1144\t      if (cached.breached) {\n1145\t        return { breached: true, count: cached.count };\n1146\t      }\n1147\t      // If cached as not breached, we still need to check if our suffix is in the list\n1148\t      // because the prefix can have multiple suffixes with different breach counts\n1149\t    }\n1150\t\n1151\t    // Query HIBP API\n1152\t    const response = await fetch(`https://api.pwnedpasswords.com/range/${prefix}`, {\n1153\t      method: \"GET\",\n1154\t      headers: {\n1155\t        \"User-Agent\": \"MTA-My-Way-Server/1.0\",\n1156\t      },\n1157\t    });\n1158\t\n1159\t    if (!response.ok) {\n1160\t      logger.warn(\"Failed to check breached password\", { status: response.status });\n1161\t      return { breached: false, count: 0 };\n1162\t    }\n1163\t\n1164\t    const body = await response.text();\n1165\t    const lines = body.split(\"\\n\");\n1166\t\n1167\t suffix.toUpperCase()) {\n1171\t        const count = parseInt(countStr ?? \"0\", 10);\n1172\t\n1173\t        // Cache the result\n1174\t        breachedPasswordCache.set(prefix, {\n1175\t          breached: true,\n1176\t          count,\n1177\t          expiresAt: now + BREACHED_PASSWORD_CACHE_TTL_MS,\n1178\t        });\n1179\t\n1180\t        return { breached: true, count };\n1181\t      }\n1182\t    }\n1183\t\n1184\t    // Cache the not-breached result\n1185\t    breachedPasswordCache.set(prefix, {\n1186\t      breached: false,\n1187\t      count: 0,\n1188\t      expiresAt: now + BREACHED_PASSWORD_CACHE_TTL_MS,\n1189\t    });\n1190\t\n1191\t    return { breached: false, count: 0 };\n1192\t  } catch (error) {\n1193\t    logger.warn(\"Error checking breached password\", error as Error);\n1194\t    return { breached: false, count: 0 };\n1195\t  }\n1196\t}\n1197\t\n1198\t/**\n1199\t * Clear the breached password cache.\n1200\t *\n1201\t * This can be useful for testing or if you want to force fresh checks.\n1202\t */\n1203\texport function clearBreachedPasswordCache(): void {\n1204\t  breachedPasswordCache.clear();\n1205\t  logger.info(\"Breached password cache cleared\");\n1206\t}\n1207\t\n1208\t// ============================================================================\n1209\t// Password Hashing\n1210\t// ============================================================================\n1211\t\n1212\t/**\n1213\t * Hash a password using Argon2id.\n1214\t *\n1215\t * Argon2id is the winner of the Password Hashing Competition (2015)\n1216\t * and is recommended by OWASP for new applications.\n1217\t *\n1218\t * Uses OWASP 2024 recommended parameters:\n1219\t * - Memory: 64 MiB\n1220\t * - Iterations: 3\n1221\t * - Parallelism: 4\n1222\t * - Salt length: 32 bytes\n1223\t * - Output length: 32 bytes\n1224\t *\n1225\t * @param password - The password to hash\n1226\t * @returns Promise containing the hash data\n1227\t */\n1228\texport async function hashPassword(password: string): Promise<PasswordHash> {\n1229\t  // Validate password is not empty\n1230\t  if (!password || password.length === 0) {\n1231\t    throw new Error(\"Password cannot be empty\");\n1232\t  }\n1233\t\n1234\t  // Combine password with pepper for additional security (if configured)\n1235\t  const pepper = getPasswordPepper();\n1236\t  const passwordWithPepper = pepper ? password + pepper : password;\n1237\t\n1238\t  // Hash using Argon2id with OWASP 2024 recommended parameters\n1239\t  // The argon2 hash,\n1249\t    salt,\n1250\t    algorithm: \"argon2id\",\n1251\t    iterations: ARGON2_OPTIONS.timeCost ?? 3,\n1252\t    memoryCost: ARGON2_OPTIONS.memoryCost,\n1253\t    parallelism: async function verifyPasswordHash(\n1269\t  password: string,\n1270\t  hash: string,\n1271\t  salt: string\n1272\t): Promise<boolean> {\n1273\t  // Validate inputs\n1274\t  if (!password || password.length === 0) {\n1275\t    return false;\n1276\t  }\n1277\t  if (!hash) {\n1278\t    return false;\n1279\t  }\n1280\t\n1281\t  try {\n1282\t    // Combine password with pepper for false\n1290\t    logger.warn(\"Password verification failed\", { error: error as Error });\n1291\t    return false;\n1292\t  }\n1293\t}\n1294\t\n1295\t/**\n1296\t * Store a password in history for a [];\n1304\t  const entry: PasswordHistoryEntry = {\n1305\t    hash,\n1306\t    salt,\n1307\t    timestamp: Date.now(),\n1308\t  };\n1309\t  history.push(entry);\n1310\t\n1311\t  // Keep only the last N passwords\n1312\t  if (history.length > DEFAULT_PASSWORD_POLICY.passwordHistoryCount) {\n1313\t    history.shift();\n1314\t  }\n1315\t\n1316\t  passwordHistory.set(keyId, history);\n1317\t}\n1318\t\n1319\t/**\n1320\t * Get password history for a key.\n1321\t *\n1322\t * @param keyId - The key ID\n1323\t * @returns Array of password history entries\n1324\t */\n1325\texport function getPasswordHistory(keyId: string): PasswordHistoryEntry[] {\n1326\t  return passwordHistory.get(keyId) ?? [];\n1327\t}\n1328\t\n1329\t/**\n1330\t * Clear password history for a key.\n1331\t *\n1332\t * @param keyId - The key ID\n1333\t * @returns Number of entries cleared\n1334\t */\n1335\texport function clearPasswordHistory(keyId: string): number {\n1336\t  const history = passwordHistory.get(keyId);\n1337\t  if (!history) return 0;\n1338\t  const count = history.length;\n1339\t  passwordHistory.delete(keyId);\n1340\t  return count;\n1341\t}\n1342\t\n1343\t// ============================================================================\n1344\t// Password Reset Flow\n1345\t// ============================================================================\n1346\t\n1347\t/**\n1348\t * Rate limit password validation attempts to prevent enumeration attacks.\n1349\t * @private Reserved for future use\n1350\t */\n1351\tfunction _checkPasswordValidationRateLimit(clientIp: string): boolean {\n1352\t  const now = Date.now();\n1353\t  const record = passwordValidationAttempts.get(clientIp);\n1354\t\n1355\t  if (!record || now > record.resetAt) {\n1356\t    passwordValidationAttempts.set(clientIp, {\n1357\t      count: 1,\n1358\t      resetAt: now + PASSWORD_VALIDATION_WINDOW_MS,\n1359\t    });\n1360\t    return true;\n1361\t  }\n1362\t\n1363\t  if (record.count >= MAX_PASSWORD_VALIDATIONS_PER_MINUTE) {\n1364\t    return false;\n1365\t  }\n1366\t\n1367\t  record.count++;\n1368\t  return true;\n1369\t}\n1370\t\n1371\t/**\n1372\t * Generate a device fingerprint from user agent for token verification.\n1373\t */\n1374\tasync function generateDeviceFingerprint(userAgent?: string): Promise<string> {\n1375\t  if (!userAgent) return \"unknown\";\n1376\t  const encoder = new TextEncoder();\n1377\t  const data = user agent.\n1388\t */\n1389\texport function getDeviceInfo(userAgent?: string): {\n1390\t  deviceType: string;\n1391\t  browser: string;\n1392\t  os: string;\n1393\t} {\n1394\t  if (!userAgent) {\n1395\t    return { deviceType: \"Unknown\", browser: \"Unknown\", os: \"Unknown\" };\n1396\t  }\n1397\t\n1398\t  const ua = userAgent.toLowerCase();\n1399\t\n1400\t  // Detect device type\n1401\t \"password12\",\n    \"password!\",\n    \"1234567890\",\n    \"1234567\",\n    \"123123\",\n    \"000000\",\n    \"111111\",\n    \"888888\",\n    \"1234\",\n    \"12345\",\n    \"12345678910\",\n    \"qwertyuiop\",\n    \"asdfgh\",\n    \"zxcvbnm\",\n    \"1q2w3e4r\",\n    \"1qaz2wsx\",\n    \"zaq12wsx\",\n    \"qwer1234\",\n    \"qwe123\",\n    \"asdf1234\",\n    // Additional weak patterns\n    \"aaaaaaaa\",\n    \"bbbbbbbb\",\n    \"cccccccc\",\n    \"dddddddd\",\n    \"eeeeeeee\",\n    \"abcd1234\",\n    \"test1234\",\n    \"temp1234\",\n    \"guest123\",\n    \"user123\",\n  ],\n  maxRepetition: 3,\n  checkBreachedPasswords: true,\n  maxBreachedCount: 0,\n  allowSpaces: true,\n  passwordExpirationDays: 0,\n  passwordHistoryCount: 12,\n  blockSequentialChars: true,\n  maxSequentialChars: 3,\n  blockKeyboardPatterns: true,\n  minStrengthScore: 40,\n};\n\n/**\n * Common keyboard patterns to detect and block.\n * Includes both forward and reverse sequences.\n */\nconst KEYBOARD_PATTERNS = [\n  // QWERTY row\n  \"qwertyuiop\",\n  \"asdfghjkl\",\n  \"zxcvbnm\",\n  // QWERTY row (reversed)\n  \"poiuytrewq\",\n  \"lkjhgfdsa\",\n  \"mnbvcxz\",\n  // QWERTY column patterns\n  \"qaz\",\n  \"wsx\",\n  \"edc\",\n  \"rfv\",\n  \"tgb\",\n  \"yhn\",\n  \"ujm\",\n  \"ik\",\n  \"ol\",\n  \"p\",\n  // QWERTY column patterns (reversed)\n  \"zaq\",\n  \"xsw\",\n  \"cde\",\n  \"vfr\",\n  \"bgt\",\n  \"nhy\",\n  \"mju\",\n  \"ki\",\n  \"lo\",\n  // Number row\n  \"1234567890\",\n  \"0987654321\",\n  // Common keyboard walking sequences (longer)\n  \"qwerty\",\n  \"asdfgh\",\n  \"zxcvbn\",\n  \"qwer\",\n  \"asdf\",\n  \"zxcv\",\n  // Reversed common sequences\n  \"ytrewq\",\n  \"hgfdsa\",\n  \"nbvcxz\",\n  // Diagonal patterns\n  \"1qaz\",\n  \"2wsx\",\n  \"3edc\",\n  \"4rfv\",\n  \"5tgb\",\n  \"6yhn\",\n  \"7ujm\",\n  \"8ik\",\n  \"9ol\",\n  \"0p\",\n  // Reversed diagonal\n  \"zaq1\",\n  \"xsw2\",\n  \"cde3\",\n  \"vfr4\",\n  \"bgt5\",\n  \"nhy6\",\n  \"mju7\",\n  \"ki8\",\n  \"lo9\",\n  \"p0\",\n];\n\n/**\n * Argon2id parameters (OWASP 2024 recommendations).\n * - Memory: 64 MiB (65536 KiB)\n * - Iterations: 3\n * - Parallelism: 4\n * - Salt length: 32 bytes\n * - Output length: 32 bytes\n */\nconst ARGON2_OPTIONS: argon2.Options = {\n  memoryCost: 65536, // 64 MiB in KiB\n  timeCost: 3, // Number of iterations\n  parallelism: 4, // Number of threads/lanes\n  hashLength: 32, // Output hash length in bytes\n  type: argon2.argon2id, // Argon2id (recommended for password hashing)\n};\n\n/**\n * PBKDF2 parameters (OWASP 2024 recommendations).\n * - Iterations: 600,000\n * - Hash: SHA-256\n * - Salt length: 32 bytes\n * - Output length: 32 bytes\n *\n * NOTE: PBKDF2 is kept for backward compatibility with existing hashes.\n * New passwords should use Argon2id.\n */\nconst PBKDF2_ITERATIONS = 600_000;\nconst PBKDF2_HASH_LENGTH = 32;\n\n/**\n * Password reset token configuration.\n */\nconst RESET_TOKEN_TTL_MS = 60 * 60 * 1000; // 1 hour\nconst RESET_TOKEN_LENGTH = 32; // bytes\n\n/**\n * Password validation rate limiting.\n */\nconst PASSWORD_VALIDATION_WINDOW_MS = 60 * 1000; // 1 minute\nconst MAX_PASSWORD_VALIDATIONS_PER_MINUTE = 10;\n\n/**\n * Password reset attempt tracking configuration.\n * Tracks failed reset attempts to prevent brute force attacks.\n */\nconst RESET_ATTEMPT_WINDOW_MS = 15 * 60 * 1000; // 15 minutes\nconst MAX_RESET_ATTEMPTS = 5; // Maximum attempts before lockout\nconst ACCOUNT_LOCKOUT_DURATION_MS = 30 * 60 * 1000; // 30 minutes\n\n/**\n * Token cleanup interval.\n * Runs periodic cleanup of expired tokens.\n */\nconst TOKEN_CLEANUP_INTERVAL_MS = 5 * 60 * 1000; // 5 minutes\n\n// ============================================================================\n// In-Memory Storage (Replace with database in production)\n// ============================================================================\n\nconst passwordResetTokens = new Map<string, PasswordResetToken>();\nconst passwordHistory = new Map<string, PasswordHistoryEntry[]>();\nconst passwordValidationAttempts = new Map<string, { count: number; resetAt: number }>();\n\n/**\n * Password reset attempt tracking.\n * Tracks failed reset attempts per email/IP combination to prevent brute force.\n * Key format: \"email:ip\" or \"email\" for IP-agnostic tracking\n */\nconst passwordResetAttempts = new Map<\n  string,\n  { count: number; resetAt: number; lockedUntil?: number }\n>();\n\n/**\n * Account lockout tracking.\n * Tracks accounts that are temporarily locked due to suspicious activity.\n */\nconst accountLockouts = new Map<\n  string,\n  { lockedUntil: number; reason: string; attempts: number }\n>();\n\n/**\n * Token cleanup interval reference.\n */\nlet tokenCleanupInterval: ReturnType<typeof setInterval> | null = null;\n\n/**\n * Breached password cache to reduce API calls.\n * Stores password hash prefixes that have been checked.\n */\nconst breachedPasswordCache = new Map<\n  string,\n  { breached: boolean; count: number; expiresAt: number }\n>();\n\n/**\n * Cache TTL for breached password results (1 hour).\n * Passwords that change breach status frequently should be re-checked.\n */\nconst BREACHED_PASSWORD_CACHE_TTL_MS = 60 * 60 * 1000;\n\n/**\n * Pepper for additional password security.\n * In production, this should be stored securely (e.g., in a secrets manager)\n * and loaded via environment variable or secure configuration.\n *\n * The pepper is a server-wide secret that is combined with the password\n * before hashing. This provides defense in depth even if the database\n * is compromised, as the attacker would also need the pepper.\n *\n * @see https://cheatsheetseries.owasp.org/cheatsheets/Password_Storage_Cheat_Sheet.html\n */\nlet PASSWORD_PEPPER = \"\";\n\n/**\n * Set the password pepper for additional security.\n *\n * IMPORTANT: In production, this should be loaded from a secure source\n * like a secrets manager or environment variable. Never hardcode the pepper.\n *\n * @param pepper - The pepper value to use (hex encoded string), or empty string to disable\n */\nexport function setPasswordPepper(pepper: string): void {\n  // Allow empty string to disable pepper\n  if (pepper === \"\") {\n    PASSWORD_PEPPER = \"\";\n    logger.info(\"Password pepper disabled\");\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Validate pepper is a valid hex string\n  if (!/^[a-fA-F0-9]+$/.test(pepper)) {\n    throw new Error(\"Password pepper must be a hex string\");\n  }\n  if (pepper.length < 32) {\n    throw new Error(\"Password pepper must be at least 16 bytes (32 hex chars)\");\n  }\n  PASSWORD_PEPPER = pepper;\n  logger.info(\"Password pepper configured\");\n}\n\n/**\n * Get the current password pepper.\n * Returns an empty string if not configured.\n *\n * @internal\n */\nfunction getPasswordPepper(): string {\n  return PASSWORD_PEPPER;\n}\n\n// ============================================================================\n// Password Reset Attempt Tracking & Account Lockout\n// ============================================================================\n\n/**\n * Check if an account is currently locked due to too many failed reset attempts.\n *\n * @param email - The email address to check\n * @returns Object indicating if locked and when it will be unlocked\n */\nexport function isAccountLocked(email: string): {\n  locked: boolean;\n  reason?: string;\n  unlockTime?: number;\n  remainingMinutes?: number;\n} {\n  const normalizedEmail = email.toLowerCase();\n  const lockout = accountLockouts.get(normalizedEmail);\n\n  if (!lockout) {\n    return { locked: false };\n  }\n\n  // Check if lockout has expired\n  if (Date.now() > lockout.lockedUntil) {\n    accountLockouts.delete(normalizedEmail);\n    passwordResetAttempts.delete(normalizedEmail);\n    return { locked: false };\n  }\n\n  const remainingMinutes = Math.ceil((lockout.lockedUntil - Date.now()) / (60 * 1000));\n\n  return {\n    locked: true,\n    reason: lockout.reason,\n    unlockTime: lockout.lockedUntil,\n    remainingMinutes,\n  };\n}\n\n/**\n * Record a failed password reset attempt.\n * Tracks attempts and implements account lockout after too many failures.\n *\n * @param email - The email address\n * @param clientIp - The client IP address\n * @returns Object indicating if account is now locked and details\n */\nexport function recordFailedResetAttempt(\n  email: string,\n  clientIp: string\n): {\n  locked: boolean;\n  attemptCount: number;\n  remainingAttempts: number;\n  lockedUntil?: number;\n} {\n  const normalizedEmail = email.toLowerCase();\n  const key = `${normalizedEmail}:${clientIp}`;\n  const now = Date.now();\n\n  let attempt = passwordResetAttempts.get(key);\n\n  // Reset if window has expired\n  if (!attempt || now > attempt.resetAt) {\n    attempt = { count: 0, resetAt: now + RESET_ATTEMPT_WINDOW_MS };\n  }\n\n  attempt.count++;\n  passwordResetAttempts.set(key, attempt);\n\n  // Also track IP-agnostic attempts (same email from any IP)\n  let globalAttempt = passwordResetAttempts.get(normalizedEmail);\n  if (!globalAttempt || now > globalAttempt.resetAt) {\n    globalAttempt = { count: 0, resetAt: now + RESET_ATTEMPT_WINDOW_MS };\n  }\n  globalAttempt.count++;\n  passwordResetAttempts.set(normalizedEmail, globalAttempt);\n\n  const remainingAttempts = Math.max(0, MAX_RESET_ATTEMPTS - globalAttempt.count);\n\n  // Check if we should lock the account\n  if (globalAttempt.count >= MAX_RESET_ATTEMPTS) {\n    const lockedUntil = now + ACCOUNT_LOCKOUT_DURATION_MS;\n    accountLockouts.set(normalizedEmail, {\n      lockedUntil,\n      reason: \"Too many failed password reset attempts\",\n      attempts: globalAttempt.count,\n    });\n\n    logger.warn(\"Account locked due to too many failed reset attempts\", {\n      email: normalizedEmail,\n      clientIp,\n      attempts: globalAttempt.count,\n      lockedUntil: new Date(lockedUntil).toISOString(),\n    });\n\n    return {\n      locked: true,\n      attemptCount: globalAttempt.count,\n      remainingAttempts: 0,\n      lockedUntil,\n    };\n  }\n\n  return {\n    locked: false,\n    attemptCount: globalAttempt.count,\n    remainingAttempts,\n  };\n}\n\n/**\n * Clear failed reset attempts for an email (e.g., after successful reset).\n *\n * @param email - The email address\n */\nexport function clearFailedResetAttempts(email: string): void {\n  const normalizedEmail = email.toLowerCase();\n\n  // Remove all entries that start with this email\n  for (const key of passwordResetAttempts.keys()) {\n    if (key === normalizedEmail || key.startsWith(`${normalizedEmail}:`)) {\n      passwordResetAttempts.delete(key);\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Also remove from lockouts\n  accountLockouts.delete(normalizedEmail);\n}\n\n/**\n * Get current failed reset attempt count for an email/IP combination.\n *\n * @param email - The email address\n * @param clientIp - The client IP address\n * @returns Number of failed attempts\n */\nexport function getFailedResetAttemptCount(email: string, clientIp: string): number {\n  const normalizedEmail = email.toLowerCase();\n  const key = `${normalizedEmail}:${clientIp}`;\n  const attempt = passwordResetAttempts.get(key);\n\n  if (!attempt || Date.now() > attempt.resetAt) {\n    return 0;\n  }\n\n  return attempt.count;\n}\n\n/**\n * Start the automatic token cleanup interval.\n * Removes expired tokens periodically to prevent memory leaks.\n *\n * @internal\n */\nexport function _startTokenCleanup(): void {\n  if (tokenCleanupInterval) {\n    return; // Already running\n  }\n\n  tokenCleanupInterval = setInterval(() => {\n    const now = Date.now();\n    let cleaned = 0;\n\n    for (const [tokenId, tokenData] of passwordResetTokens.entries()) {\n      // Remove expired or used tokens\n      if (now > tokenData.expiresAt || tokenData.used) {\n        passwordResetTokens.delete(tokenId);\n        cleaned++;\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Clean expired lockouts\n    for (const [email, lockout] of accountLockouts.entries()) {\n      if (now > lockout.lockedUntil) {\n        accountLockouts.delete(email);\n        passwordResetAttempts.delete(email);\n      }\n    }\n\n    if (cleaned > 0) {\n      logger.debug(\"Token cleanup completed\", { cleaned, remaining: passwordResetTokens.size });\n    }\n  }, TOKEN_CLEANUP_INTERVAL_MS);\n\n  logger.info(\"Token cleanup interval started\", { intervalMs: TOKEN_CLEANUP_INTERVAL_MS });\n}\n\n/**\n * Stop the automatic token cleanup interval.\n *\n * @internal\n */\nexport function _stopTokenCleanup(): void {\n  if (tokenCleanupInterval) {\n    clearInterval(tokenCleanupInterval);\n    tokenCleanupInterval = null;\n    logger.info(\"Token cleanup interval stopped\");\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Manually trigger token cleanup.\n * Useful for testing or immediate cleanup.\n *\n * @returns Number of tokens cleaned up\n */\nexport function cleanupExpiredTokens(): number {\n  const now = Date.now();\n  let cleaned = 0;\n\n  for (const [tokenId, tokenData] of passwordResetTokens.entries()) {\n    if (now > tokenData.expiresAt || tokenData.used) {\n      passwordResetTokens.delete(tokenId);\n      cleaned++;\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Clean expired lockouts\n  for (const [email, lockout] of accountLockouts.entries()) {\n    if (now > lockout.lockedUntil) {\n      accountLockouts.delete(email);\n      passwordResetAttempts.delete(email);\n    }\n  }\n\n  return cleaned;\n}\n\n// ============================================================================\n// Password Validation\n// ============================================================================\n\n/**\n * Detect sequential character patterns in password.\n * Checks for:\n * - Numeric sequences: 1234, 4321, 0123\n * - Alphabetic sequences: abcd, DCBA, mnop\n * - Both forward and reverse sequences\n *\n * @param password - The password to check\n * @param maxSequence - Maximum allowed sequential characters\n * @returns Object indicating if sequential pattern was found and the pattern\n */\nfunction detectSequentialChars(\n  password: string,\n  maxSequence: number\n): { found: boolean; pattern?: string } {\n  const lowerPassword = password.toLowerCase();\n\n  // Check each position for sequences\n  for (let i = 0; i < lowerPassword.length - (maxSequence - 1); i++) {\n    // Extract potential sequence\n    const sequence = lowerPassword.substring(i, i + maxSequence + 1);\n\n    // Check if it's a valid sequence (all letters or all digits)\n    const isAllLetters = /^[a-z]+$/.test(sequence);\n    const isAllDigits = /^\\d+$/.test(sequence);\n\n    if (!isAllLetters && !isAllDigits) {\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    // Check for forward or reverse sequential pattern\n    if (isSequentialSequence(sequence)) {\n      return { found: true, pattern: sequence };\n    }\n  }\n\n  return { found: false };\n}\n\n/**\n * Check if a string is a sequential character pattern.\n * Handles both forward (abcd, 1234) and reverse (dcba, 4321) sequences.\n */\nfunction isSequentialSequence(str: string): boolean {\n  if (str.length < 2) return false;\n\n  // Check forward sequence\n  let isForward = true;\n  let isReverse = true;\n\n  for (let i = 0; i < str.length - 1; i++) {\n    const current = str.charCodeAt(i);\n    const next = str.charCodeAt(i + 1);\n\n    // Forward: next char is exactly +1\n    if (next !== current + 1) {\n      isForward = false;\n    }\n\n    // Reverse: next char is exactly -1\n    if (next !== current - 1) {\n      isReverse = false;\n    }\n  }\n\n  return isForward || isReverse;\n}\n\n/**\n * Detect keyboard walking patterns in password.\n * Checks for common keyboard sequences like \"qwerty\", \"asdf\", \"1qaz\", etc.\n *\n * Only reports patterns of 3+ characters to avoid false positives on\n * single characters that happen to be part of keyboard layouts.\n *\n * @param password - The password to check\n * @returns Object indicating if keyboard pattern was found and the pattern\n */\nfunction detectKeyboardPatterns(password: string): { found: boolean; pattern?: string } {\n  const lowerPassword = password.toLowerCase();\n  const MIN_PATTERN_LENGTH = 3;\n\n  // Check each pattern\n  for (const pattern of KEYBOARD_PATTERNS) {\n    // Skip patterns shorter than minimum length\n    if (pattern.length < MIN_PATTERN_LENGTH) {\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    // Check if pattern exists in password (case-insensitive)\n    if (lowerPassword.includes(pattern)) {\n      return { found: true, pattern };\n    }\n\n    // Also check reversed version of pattern\n    const reversed = pattern.split(\"\").reverse().join(\"\");\n    if (lowerPassword.includes(reversed)) {\n      return { found: true, pattern: reversed };\n    }\n  }\n\n  return { found: false };\n}\n\n/**\n * Detect common password variations like \"password1\", \"password2\", etc.\n *\n * @param password - The password to check\n * @param skipKeyboardBased - Whether to skip keyboard-based common words (when blockKeyboardPatterns is false)\n * @returns Object indicating if common variation was found\n */\nfunction detectCommonVariations(\n  password: string,\n  skipKeyboardBased = false\n): { found: boolean; pattern?: string } {\n  const lowerPassword = password.toLowerCase();\n\n  // Common base passwords with number/special char variations\n  // Keyboard-based words (qwerty, asdf) are skipped when blockKeyboardPatterns is false\n  const commonBases = [\n    \"password\",\n    \"passw0rd\",\n    \"admin\",\n    \"welcome\",\n    \"login\",\n    // Skip keyboard-based words when requested\n    ...(skipKeyboardBased ? [] : [\"qwerty\"]),\n    \"letmein\",\n    \"monkey\",\n    \"dragon\",\n    \"master\",\n  ];\n\n  for (const base of commonBases) {\n    // Check if password starts with common base\n    if (!lowerPassword.startsWith(base)) {\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    const suffix = lowerPassword.slice(base.length);\n\n    // If there's no suffix, it's just the base word (handled elsewhere)\n    if (suffix.length === 0) {\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    // Check if suffix is only numbers\n    if (/^\\d+$/.test(suffix)) {\n      return { found: true, pattern: base + \"[numbers]\" };\n    }\n\n    // Check if suffix is only special characters\n    if (/^[!@#$%^&*]+$/.test(suffix)) {\n      return { found: true, pattern: base + \"[special]\" };\n    }\n\n    // Check if suffix is a year (19xx or 20xx)\n    if (/^(19\\d\\d|20\\d\\d)$/.test(suffix)) {\n      return { found: true, pattern: base + \"[year]\" };\n    }\n\n    // Check if suffix is numbers followed by special chars (e.g., \"password123!@#\")\n    if (/^\\d+[!@#$%^&*]+$/.test(suffix)) {\n      return { found: true, pattern: base + \"[numbers+special]\" };\n    }\n\n    // Check if suffix is special chars followed by numbers (e.g., \"password!@#123\")\n    if (/^[!@#$%^&*]+\\d+$/.test(suffix)) {\n      return { found: true, pattern: base + \"[special+numbers]\" };\n    }\n\n    // Check if suffix is a year followed by special chars (e.g., \"password2024!@#\")\n    if (/^(19\\d\\d|20\\d\\d)[!@#$%^&*]+$/.test(suffix)) {\n      return { found: true, pattern: base + \"[year+special]\" };\n    }\n  }\n\n  return { found: false };\n}\n\n/**\n * Validate a password against policy requirements.\n *\n * This function performs comprehensive password validation including:\n * - Length requirements\n * - Character complexity\n * - Common password detection\n * - Character repetition\n * - Breached password checking (via HIBP k-anonymity API)\n * - Password strength scoring\n *\n * @param password - The password to validate\n * @param policy - Optional custom policy (uses defaults if not provided)\n * @param keyId - Optional key ID for password history checking\n * @returns Validation result with detailed feedback\n */\nexport async function validatePassword(\n  password: string,\n  policy: PasswordPolicy = {},\n  keyId?: string\n): Promise<PasswordValidationResult> {\n  const mergedPolicy = { ...DEFAULT_PASSWORD_POLICY, ...policy };\n  const errors: string[] = [];\n\n  // Check maximum length FIRST before any sanitization\n  // This ensures we catch long passwords and provide a clear error message\n  if (password.length > mergedPolicy.maxLength) {\n    errors.push(`Password must be no more than ${mergedPolicy.maxLength} characters long`);\n    return {\n      valid: false,\n      errors,\n      strength: 0,\n      strengthCategory: \"weak\",\n    };\n  }\n\n  // Check minimum length\n  if (password.length < mergedPolicy.minLength) {\n    errors.push(`Password must be at least ${mergedPolicy.minLength} characters long`);\n  }\n\n  // Sanitize input to prevent injection attacks (without length truncation since we already checked)\n  // For passwords, we only do basic sanitization - no SQL/Command injection prevention\n  // since those would incorrectly reject valid passwords containing words like \"or\", \"and\", etc.\n  const sanitizedPassword = sanitizeStringSimple(password, {\n    maxLength: password.length, // Don't truncate, we already validated length\n    preserveCase: true,\n    preserveWhitespace: mergedPolicy.allowSpaces,\n    preventSqlInjection: false, // Don't prevent SQL injection in passwords\n    preventCommandInjection: false, // Don't prevent command injection in passwords\n    preventLdapInjection: false, // Don't prevent LDAP injection in passwords\n    preventNosqlInjection: false, // Don't prevent NoSQL injection in passwords\n  });\n\n  // Check if sanitization changed the password (injection patterns detected)\n  // We only check for XSS patterns in passwords since those are actual security risks\n  if (sanitizedPassword !== password) {\n    errors.push(\"Password contains invalid characters\");\n    return {\n      valid: false,\n      errors,\n      strength: 0,\n      strengthCategory: \"weak\",\n    };\n  }\n\n  // Check uppercase\n  if (mergedPolicy.requireUppercase && !/[A-Z]/.test(password)) {\n    errors.push(\"Password must contain at least one uppercase letter\");\n  }\n\n  // Check lowercase\n  if (mergedPolicy.requireLowercase && !/[a-z]/.test(password)) {\n    errors.push(\"Password must contain at least one lowercase letter\");\n  }\n\n  // Check numbers\n  if (mergedPolicy.requireNumbers && !/\\d/.test(password)) {\n    errors.push(\"Password must contain at least one number\");\n  }\n\n  // Check special characters\n  if (mergedPolicy.requireSpecialChars && !/[!@#$%^&*()_+\\-=[\\]{};':\"\\\\|,.<>/?]/.test(password)) {\n    errors.push(\"Password must contain at least one special character\");\n  }\n\n  // Check spaces\n  if (!mergedPolicy.allowSpaces && /\\s/.test(password)) {\n    errors.push(\"Password cannot contain spaces\");\n  }\n\n  // Check against blocked passwords (exact match only)\n  // Substring matching is too aggressive and would reject valid passwords\n  // like \"SecurePass123!\" that happen to contain common words\n  const lowerPassword = password.toLowerCase();\n  for (const blocked of mergedPolicy.blockedPasswords) {\n    if (lowerPassword === blocked) {\n      errors.push(\"Password is too common or weak\");\n      break;\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Check character repetition\n  if (mergedPolicy.maxRepetition > 0) {\n    const repetitionRegex = new RegExp(`(.)\\\\1{${mergedPolicy.maxRepetition},}`, \"g\");\n    if (repetitionRegex.test(password)) {\n      errors.push(\n        `Password cannot contain the same character more than ${mergedPolicy.maxRepetition} times in a row`\n      );\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Check sequential character patterns\n  if (mergedPolicy.blockSequentialChars && mergedPolicy.maxSequentialChars > 0) {\n    const sequentialResult = detectSequentialChars(password, mergedPolicy.maxSequentialChars);\n    if (sequentialResult.found) {\n      errors.push(\n        `Password contains sequential characters (${sequentialResult.pattern}). Avoid using patterns like \"1234\" or \"abcd\".`\n      );\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Check keyboard walking patterns\n  if (mergedPolicy.blockKeyboardPatterns) {\n    const keyboardResult = detectKeyboardPatterns(password);\n    if (keyboardResult.found) {\n      errors.push(\n        `Password contains keyboard pattern (${keyboardResult.pattern}). Avoid using keyboard sequences.`\n      );\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Check common password variations\n  // Skip keyboard-based words when blockKeyboardPatterns is disabled\n  const variationResult = detectCommonVariations(password, !mergedPolicy.blockKeyboardPatterns);\n  if (variationResult.found) {\n    errors.push(\n      `Password contains a common variation pattern (${variationResult.pattern}). Please choose a more unique password.`\n    );\n  }\n\n  // Calculate strength score\n  const strength = calculatePasswordStrength(password);\n  const strengthCategory = getStrengthCategory(strength);\n\n  // Check password history if keyId provided\n  if (keyId && mergedPolicy.passwordHistoryCount > 0) {\n    const history = passwordHistory.get(keyId);\n    if (history) {\n      // Check against recent passwords\n      const recentHistory = history.slice(-mergedPolicy.passwordHistoryCount);\n      for (const entry of recentHistory) {\n        if (await verifyPasswordHash(password, entry.hash, entry.salt)) {\n          errors.push(\"Cannot reuse a recent password\");\n          break;\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Check breached passwords via HIBP API\n  let breached = false;\n  let breachCount = 0;\n  if (mergedPolicy.checkBreachedPasswords && errors.length === 0) {\n    const breachResult = await checkBreachedPassword(password);\n    breached = breachResult.breached;\n    breachCount = breachResult.count;\n\n    if (breached && breachCount > (mergedPolicy.maxBreachedCount ?? 0)) {\n      errors.push(\n        `This password has been found in data breaches ${breachCount} times. Please choose a different password.`\n      );\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Check minimum strength score\n  if (strength < (mergedPolicy.minStrengthScore ?? 0)) {\n    errors.push(\n      `Password is too weak (strength: ${strength}/100). Please choose a stronger password.`\n    );\n  }\n\n  return {\n    valid: errors.length === 0,\n    errors,\n    strength,\n    strengthCategory,\n    breached,\n    breachCount: breached ? breachCount : undefined,\n  };\n}\n\n/**\n * Calculate password strength score (0-100).\n *\n * Uses entropy-based calculation with bonuses for:\n * - Length\n * - Character variety\n * - Character distribution\n */\nfunction calculatePasswordStrength(password: string): number {\n  let score = 0;\n\n  // Length score (up to 40 points)\n  score += Math.min(40, password.length * 2);\n\n  // Character variety (up to 30 points)\n  if (/[a-z]/.test(password)) score += 5;\n  if (/[A-Z]/.test(password)) score += 5;\n  if (/\\d/.test(password)) score += 5;\n  if (/[!@#$%^&*()_+\\-=[\\]{};':\"\\\\|,.<>/?]/.test(password)) score += 10;\n  if (/\\s/.test(password)) score += 5;\n\n  // Character distribution (up to 20 points)\n  const uniqueChars = new Set(password).size;\n  score += Math.min(20, (uniqueChars / password.length) * 20);\n\n  // Complexity bonus (up to 10 points)\n  const hasMixedCase = /[a-z]/.test(password) && /[A-Z]/.test(password);\n  const hasNumbers = /\\d/.test(password);\n  const hasSpecial = /[!@#$%^&*()_+\\-=\\[\\]{};':\"\\\\|,.<>\\/?]/.test(password);\n  if (hasMixedCase && hasNumbers && hasSpecial) score += 10;\n\n  return Math.min(100, score);\n}\n\n/**\n * Get strength category from score.\n */\nfunction getStrengthCategory(score: number): \"weak\" | \"fair\" | \"good\" | \"strong\" {\n  if (score < 40) return \"weak\";\n  if (score < 60) return \"fair\";\n  if (score < 80) return \"good\";\n  return \"strong\";\n}\n\n/**\n * Check if a password has been breached using Have I Been Pwned k-anonymity API.\n *\n * Uses the k-anonymity model where only the first 5 characters of the\n * SHA-256 hash are sent to the API. The full hash never leaves the server.\n *\n * Results are cached for 1 hour to reduce API calls and improve performance.\n *\n * @param password - The password to check\n * @returns Object indicating Uint8Array(hashBuffer));\n    const hash = hashArray.map((b) => b.toString(16).padStart(2, \"0\")).join(\"\");\n\n    // Get first 5 characters for API request (cache key)\n    const prefix = hash.substring(0, 5);\n    const suffix = hash.substring(5);\n\n    // Check cache first\n    const cached = breachedPasswordCache.get(prefix);\n    const now = Date.now();\n    if (cached && now < cached.expiresAt) {\n      // Check if our specific suffix matches\n      if (cached.breached) {\n        return { breached: true, count: cached.count };\n      }\n      // If cached as not breached,     logger.warn(\"Failed to check breached password\", { status: response.status });\n      return { breached: false, count: 0 };\n    }\n\n    const body = await response.text();\n    const lines = body.split(\"\\n\");\n\n    // Check if our suffix is in the results\n    for (const line of lines) {\n      const [lineSuffix, countStr] = line.split(\":\");\n      if (lineSuffix?.toUpperCase() === suffix.toUpperCase()) {\n        const count = parseInt(countStr ?? \"0\", 10);\n\n        // Cache the result\n        breachedPasswordCache.set(prefix, {\n          breached: true,\n breachedPasswordCache.set(prefix, {\n      breached: false,\n      count: 0,\n      expiresAt: now + BREACHED_PASSWORD_CACHE_TTL_MS,\n    });\n\n    return { breached: false, count: 0 };\n  } catch ============================================================================\n\n/**\n * Hash a password using Argon2id.\n *\n * Argon2id is the winner of the Password Hashing Competition (2015)\n * and is recommended by OWASP for new applications.\n *\n * Uses OWASP 2024 recommended parameters:\n * - Memory: 64 MiB\n * - Iterations: 3\n * - Parallelism: 4\n * - Salt length: 32 bytes\n * - Output
